The `validatingDispatcher` struct in dispatcher.go implements parallel webhook dispatch.\\n   - The `Dispatch()` method first collects all relevant webhooks (filtering by selectors and rules), then spawns goroutines for parallel webhook calls, each invoking `callHook()`.\\n   - The parallel dispatch pattern uses `sync.WaitGroup` and error channels to manage concurrent webhook invocations and collect errors.\\n   - The `Plugin` struct (in plugin.go) wraps `Webhook` and implements the `Validate()` interface method.\\n\\n4. **WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer** (kubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go)\\n   - The `WebhookAccessor` interface provides a unified way to access both mutating and validating webhook configuration.\\n   - It abstracts away the differences between `v1.MutatingWebhook` and `v1.ValidatingWebhook` API types.\\n   - Key methods: `GetUID()`, `GetName()`, `GetConfigurationName()`, `GetRules()`, `GetFailurePolicy()`, `GetRESTClient()`, `GetCompiledMatcher()`, `GetMutatingWebhook()`, `GetValidatingWebhook()`.\\n   - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` is a cluster-scoped resource containing a list of mutating webhooks.\\n   - `MutatingWebhook` defines a single mutating webhook with fields: Name, ClientConfig, Rules, FailurePolicy, SideEffects, TimeoutSeconds, AdmissionReviewVersions, NamespaceSelector, ObjectSelector, MatchPolicy, ReinvocationPolicy, and MatchConditions.\\n   - `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` is a cluster-scoped resource containing a list of validating webhooks.\\n   - `ValidatingWebhook` defines a single validating webhook with similar fields (minus ReinvocationPolicy).\\n   - Key shared types: `FailurePolicyType` (Ignore/Fail), `SideEffectClass`, `MatchPolicyType` (Exact/Equivalent), `RuleWithOperations`, and `MatchCondition`.\\n\\nThe processing chain flows as follows: When an API request arrives, either the `mutating.Plugin.Admit()` or `validating.Plugin.Validate()` method is called. These delegate to `Webhook.Dispatch()`, which retrieves configured webhooks and calls the type-specific dispatcher. For mutating webhooks, `mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` processes webhooks sequentially, applying patches and tracking mutations via `webhookReinvokeContext` for potential reinvocation. For validating webhooks, `validatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` filters webhooks then spawns parallel goroutines for concurrent validation. Both dispatcher types use `Webhook.ShouldCallHook()` to evaluate webhook applicability via the `WebhookAccessor` interface, which abstracts the underlying v1.MutatingWebhook and v1.ValidatingWebhook API objects from `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` and `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` resources.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":365,"cache_read_input_tokens":59986,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":365},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"8dc8a907-826d-4273-9fc9-92254b6464ea","uuid":"a339925f-7ea5-40c4-bc3c-f49e40a6d327"}

The architecture is organized in layers:\\n\\n1. **Generic Webhook Foundation** (kubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/)\\n   - The `Webhook` struct in webhook.go serves as the abstract dispatcher that coordinates webhook admission checks.\\n   - The `NewWebhook()` function initializes a generic webhook with a dispatcher factory pattern, allowing different implementations for mutating and validating webhooks.\\n   - The `Dispatch()` method retrieves hooks from a source and delegates to specific dispatcher implementations.\\n   - The `ShouldCallHook()` method evaluates whether a specific webhook should be called based on namespace/object selectors and match rules.\\n   - Key interfaces defined in interfaces.go: `Dispatcher` (for dispatching requests), `Source` (for listing webhooks), `WebhookInvocation` (describing how to call a webhook), and `VersionedAttributeAccessor` (for versioning admission attributes).\\n\\n2. **Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic** (kubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/)\\n   - The `mutatingDispatcher` struct in dispatcher.go implements sequential webhook dispatch with mutation tracking.\\n   - The `Dispatch()` method iterates through webhooks sequentially and tracks mutation state via `webhookReinvokeContext`.\\n   - The `callAttrMutatingHook()` method handles the actual webhook invocation, patch application, and object mutation.\\n   - The `webhookAnnotator` tracks audit annotations for patches, mutations, and failed-open scenarios.\\n   - `webhookReinvokeContext` (in reinvocationcontext.go) implements reinvocation logic: it tracks previously invoked webhooks with ReinvocationPolicy=IfNeeded, detects when objects are mutated by in-tree plugins, and re-invokes eligible webhooks. Methods include `ShouldReinvokeWebhook()`, `IsOutputChangedSinceLastWebhookInvocation()`, and `RequireReinvokingPreviouslyInvokedPlugins()`.\\n   - The `Plugin` struct (in plugin.go) wraps `Webhook` and implements the `Admit()` interface method, which calls `Webhook.Dispatch()`.\\n   - Audit annotations include `MutationAuditAnnotation` and `PatchAuditAnnotation` for tracking mutations and patches applied.\\n\\n3. **Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch** (kubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/)\\n   - The `validatingDispatcher` struct in dispatcher.go implements parallel webhook dispatch.\\n   - The `Dispatch()` method first collects all relevant webhooks (filtering by selectors and rules), then spawns goroutines for parallel webhook calls, each invoking `callHook()`.\\n   - The parallel dispatch pattern uses `sync.WaitGroup` and error channels to manage concurrent webhook invocations and collect errors.\\n   - The `Plugin` struct (in plugin.go) wraps `Webhook` and implements the `Validate()` interface method.\\n\\n4. **WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer** (kubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go)\\n   - The `WebhookAccessor` interface provides a unified way to access both mutating and validating webhook configuration.\\n   - It abstracts away the differences between `v1.MutatingWebhook` and `v1.ValidatingWebhook` API types.\\n   - Key methods: `GetUID()`, `GetName()`, `GetConfigurationName()`, `GetRules()`, `GetFailurePolicy()`, `GetRESTClient()`, `GetCompiledMatcher()`, `GetMutatingWebhook()`, `GetValidatingWebhook()`.\\n   - Two implementations: `mutatingWebhookAccessor` and `validatingWebhookAccessor` wrap the corresponding API objects.\\n   - Both accessors use sync.Once for lazy initialization of REST clients, selectors, and compiled match conditions.\\n   - Factory functions `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` create accessor instances.\\n\\n5. **API Type Definitions** (kubernetes/api: admissionregistration/v1/types.go)\\n   - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` is a cluster-scoped resource containing a list of mutating webhooks.\\n   - `MutatingWebhook` defines a single mutating webhook with fields: Name, ClientConfig, Rules, FailurePolicy, SideEffects, TimeoutSeconds, AdmissionReviewVersions, NamespaceSelector, ObjectSelector, MatchPolicy, ReinvocationPolicy, and MatchConditions.\\n   - `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` is a cluster-scoped resource containing a list of validating webhooks.\\n   - `ValidatingWebhook` defines a single validating webhook with similar fields (minus ReinvocationPolicy).\\n   - Key shared types: `FailurePolicyType` (Ignore/Fail), `SideEffectClass`, `MatchPolicyType` (Exact/Equivalent), `RuleWithOperations`, and `MatchCondition`.\\n\\nThe processing chain flows as follows: When an API request arrives, either the `mutating.Plugin.Admit()` or `validating.Plugin.Validate()` method is called. These delegate to `Webhook.Dispatch()`, which retrieves configured webhooks and calls the type-specific dispatcher. For mutating webhooks, `mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` processes webhooks sequentially, applying patches and tracking mutations via `webhookReinvokeContext` for potential reinvocation. For validating webhooks, `validatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` filters webhooks then spawns parallel goroutines for concurrent validation. Both dispatcher types use `Webhook.ShouldCallHook()` to evaluate webhook applicability via the `WebhookAccessor` interface, which abstracts the underlying v1.MutatingWebhook and v1.ValidatingWebhook API objects from `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` and `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` resources.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
